DOM Event specification. Here is the complete flow:\\n\\n## 1. Event Initiation (EventDispatcher::Dispatch)\\nThe event dispatch process begins in `dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp` at line 869 with `EventDispatcher::Dispatch()`. This static method:\\n- Takes an EventTarget, WidgetEvent, optional DOM Event object, and presentation context\\n- Validates the event state to ensure it's not already being dispatched\\n- Sets the event's mTarget and mOriginalTarget based on event retargeting rules\\n- Creates performance timing entries for the event\\n\\n## 2. Event Creation (EventDispatcher::CreateEvent)\\nAt line 1419 in the same file, `EventDispatcher::CreateEvent()` creates appropriate DOM Event objects:\\n- Examines the WidgetEvent class (eMouseEventClass, eKeyboardEventClass, etc.)\\n- Dispatches to type-specific constructors (NS_NewDOMMouseEvent, NS_NewDOMKeyboardEvent, etc.)\\n- Creates vanilla Event objects for unspecified types\\n- Handles both system and web-accessible event types\\n\\n## 3. Event Target Chain Creation\\nThe dispatcher builds a chain of event targets by:\\n- Creating EventTargetChainItem objects (line 125-427 in EventDispatcher.cpp)\\n- Calling GetEventTargetParent() on each target via EventChainPreVisitor\\n- Walking up the DOM tree until reaching a target that cannot handle the event\\n- Establishing retargeting points for shadow DOM and anonymous content\\n\\n## 4. Capture Phase (lines 516-585 in HandleEventTargetChain)\\n- Sets mInCapturePhase and mInTargetPhase flags on the event\\n- Iterates from the top of the chain down to (but not including) the target\\n- Calls EventTargetChainItem::HandleEvent() on each item\\n- Respects propagation stopped flags and dispatch filters\\n\\n## 5. Target Phase (lines 587-611)\\n- Sets mInTargetPhase flag\\n- Calls HandleEvent() twice: once for capture listeners, once for bubble listeners\\n- Allows both capturing and bubbling listeners on the target element itself\\n- In system event group, calls PostHandleEvent() after each listener\\n\\n## 6. Bubble Phase (lines 613-649)\\n- Sets mInBubblingPhase flag\\n- Iterates from just after the target up to the top of the chain\\n- Calls HandleEvent() on each item that has bubbling listeners\\n- Only dispatches if event.bubbles is true (with exception for retargeting)\\n- Calls PostHandleEvent() for system group handlers\\n\\n## 7. Event Listener Invocation (EventTargetChainItem::HandleEvent)\\nAt line 339 in EventDispatcher.cpp:\\n- Calls WillHandleEvent() if needed\\n- Gets or creates the EventListenerManager from the current target\\n- Calls EventListenerManager::HandleEvent() to invoke registered listeners\\n\\n## 8. Individual Listener Invocation (EventListenerManager::HandleEventSingleListener)\\nAt line 1233 in EventListenerManager.cpp:\\n- Sets the current event on the window (if applicable)\\n- Compiles script handlers if needed\\n- Invokes WebIDL callbacks via HandleEvent() at line 1276\\n- Or invokes XPCOM listeners via HandleEvent() at line 1281-1282\\n- Manages passive listener flags and exception handling\\n\\n## 9. Default Action Execution\\nAfter all listeners are invoked:\\n- PreActivationBehavior is called before the target phase (for legacy form submissions)\\n- ActivationBehavior is called after dispatch if event.defaultPrevented() is false\\n- Examples: HTMLButtonElement::ActivationBehavior() submits forms or triggers commands\\n- PostHandleEvent callbacks in the system group handle platform-specific actions\\n\\n## 10. System Event Group\\nAfter the default event group completes:\\n- If the event can dispatch in the system group (IsAllowedToDispatchInSystemGroup)\\n- Resets propagation flags for the system group\\n- Re-dispatches through the entire capture/target/bubble chain again\\n- System group handlers run after content handlers\\n- This is used for internal Firefox event processing\\n\\n## Key Files:\\n- **dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp/h**: Core dispatch logic, event creation, target chain\\n- **dom/events/EventListenerManager.cpp/h**: Listener registration and invocation\\n- **dom/events/EventTarget.cpp/h**: Base class for event targets with activation behavior\\n- **dom/html/HTMLButtonElement.cpp**: Example implementation of default action behavior\\n\\nThe dispatch chain ensures proper event ordering (capture before bubble), listener invocation order, preventDefault() semantics, and default action execution according to the W3C DOM specification.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":8,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3297,"cache_read_input_tokens":105955,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3297},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"a48a0bbb-5a30-498d-8042-9beada01cf4c","uuid":"299efadb-c004-48fe-8c85-f10a5604c8b3"}

Here is the complete flow:\\n\\n## 1. Event Initiation (EventDispatcher::Dispatch)\\nThe event dispatch process begins in `dom/events/EventDispatcher.cpp` at line 869 with `EventDispatcher::Dispatch()`. This static method:\\n- Takes an EventTarget, WidgetEvent, optional DOM Event object, and presentation context\\n- Validates the event state to ensure it's not already being dispatched\\n- Sets the event's mTarget and mOriginalTarget based on event retargeting rules\\n- Creates performance timing entries for the event\\n\\n## 2. Event Creation (EventDispatcher::CreateEvent)\\nAt line 1419 in the same file, `EventDispatcher::CreateEvent()` creates appropriate DOM Event objects:\\n- Examines the WidgetEvent class (eMouseEventClass, eKeyboardEventClass, etc.)\\n- Dispatches to type-specific constructors (NS_NewDOMMouseEvent, NS_NewDOMKeyboardEvent, etc.)\\n- Creates vanilla Event objects for unspecified types\\n- Handles both system and web-accessible event types\\n\\n## 3. Event Target Chain Creation\\nThe dispatcher builds a chain of event targets by:\\n- Creating EventTargetChainItem objects (line 125-427 in EventDispatcher.cpp)\\n- Calling GetEventTargetParent() on each target via EventChainPreVisitor\\n- Walking up the DOM tree until reaching a target that cannot handle the event\\n- Establishing retargeting points for shadow DOM and anonymous content\\n\\n## 4. Capture Phase (lines 516-585 in HandleEventTargetChain)\\n- Sets mInCapturePhase and mInTargetPhase flags on the event\\n- Iterates from the top of the chain down to (but not including) the target\\n- Calls EventTargetChainItem::HandleEvent() on each item\\n- Respects propagation stopped flags and dispatch filters\\n\\n## 5. Target Phase (lines 587-611)\\n- Sets mInTargetPhase flag\\n- Calls HandleEvent() twice: once for capture listeners, once for bubble listeners\\n- Allows both capturing and bubbling listeners on the target element itself\\n- In system event group, calls PostHandleEvent() after each listener\\n\\n## 6. Bubble Phase (lines 613-649)\\n- Sets mInBubblingPhase flag\\n- Iterates from just after the target up to the top of the chain\\n- Calls HandleEvent() on each item that has bubbling listeners\\n- Only dispatches if event.bubbles is true (with exception for retargeting)\\n- Calls PostHandleEvent() for system group handlers\\n\\n## 7.
